namespace = daoyu
daoyu.1 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_on
	desc = daoyu_on
	flavor = daoyu_on_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_activate
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_off
		set_global_variable = daoyu_on
		set_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.2 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_off
		set_global_variable = daoyu_off
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_reconsideration
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_off
	}
}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 3
	option = {
		name = daoyu_understand
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { this = c:CHI game_date = 1836.1.1 } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.9 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}
daoyu.3 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_can_select_target_state } } set_global_variable = daoyu_can_select_target_state }
	}
}
daoyu.9 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	duration = 0
	title = warlord_china_events.200.t
	desc = daoyu_cheat
	flavor = warlord_china_events.200.f
	event_image = { video = "asia_farmers_market" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/waving_flag.dds"
	option = {
		default_option = yes
		name = daoyu_cheat
	}
	option = {
		name = dyn_c_empire_of_china
		if = {
			limit = { has_journal_entry = je_warlord_china }
			set_variable = won_boxer_rebellion set_variable = china_warlord_explosion_recognized set_variable = china_warlord_abolished_monarchy
			set_variable = { name = china_warlord_explosion value = 5 }
			if = { limit = { is_country_type = unrecognized } set_country_type = recognized }
			if = { limit = { has_law = law_type:law_monarchy } activate_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_primary_culture = cu:manchu
			every_primary_culture = { remove_cultural_obsession = opium }
			create_character = { first_name = Guofan last_name = Zeng historical = yes culture = cu:han female = no ruler = yes ideology = ideology_traditionalist interest_group = ig_armed_forces birth_date = 1811.11.26 traits = { plains_commander pious pillager } }
			random_character = { limit = { culture = cu:manchu is_heir = yes } kill_character = { hidden = yes } }
		}
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
}
daoyu.10 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = MAIN_MENU

	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { set_global_variable = daoyu_can_select_target_state }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_common
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ECONOMY#经济
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_characters#角色
		set_global_variable = daoyu_character_events
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DIPLOMACY#外交
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
			random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_cultures
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = STATES
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = LAWS
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.700 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TECHNOLOGY
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = d_law_tec.800 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = pmg_automation#自动化
		set_global_variable = daoyu_automation
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.900 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_country_desc
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.10 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_fast_construction#快速建造
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_show_daoyu_fast_construction } }
		set_variable = daoyu_show_daoyu_fast_construction
		add_journal_entry = { type = daoyu_fast_construction }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
	}
}
#常用
daoyu.100 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_common
	flavor = daoyu_common_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_enactment_advance#立法推进
		trigger = { enacting_any_law = yes }
		add_enactment_modifier = { name = daoyu_auto_law_modifier }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_credit_debt#债务
		trigger = { scaled_debt > 0.0001 }
		clear_debt = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = good_pollution_modifier#污染治理措施
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { state_region = { pollution_amount > 1 } } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { state_region = { pollution_amount > 1 } } state_region = { add_pollution = -100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_devastation#荒废度
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { devastation > 0.01 } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { devastation > 0.01 } state_region = { add_devastation = -100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = suppressing_radicals#打压激进主义者
		trigger = { radical_fraction = { value > 0 } }
		add_loyalists = { value = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_liberty_desire#独立倾向
		trigger = { any_subject_or_below = { liberty_desire > 10 } }
		every_subject_or_below = { add_liberty_desire = -100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_infamy#恶名
		trigger = { infamy >= 1 }
		change_infamy = -100
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporate_state#整合地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { is_treaty_port = no is_incorporated = no state_region = { not = { any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } } } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_treaty_port = no is_incorporated = no state_region = { not = { any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } } } set_state_type = incorporated }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_recognized_power_short#受认可
		trigger = { is_country_type = unrecognized }
		set_country_type = recognized
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = war_goal_independence#独立
		trigger = { is_subject = yes }
		make_independent = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_redeem_all_obligation#免除义务
		trigger = { any_country = { root = { owes_obligation_to = prev } } }
		every_country = { limit = { root = { owes_obligation_to = prev } } root = { set_owes_obligation_to = { country = prev setting = no } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_preventing_great_disasters#预防大灾难
		trigger = { nor = { has_variable = mega_flood has_variable = mega_earthquake has_variable = mega_eruption } }
		set_variable = mega_flood
		set_variable = mega_earthquake
		set_variable = mega_eruption
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_country_modifiers#修正
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.190 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_negative_modifiers#删除负面修正
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.195 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PRESTIGE#威望
		set_global_variable = daoyu_from_common
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.108 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_power_bloc#国家集团
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.130 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_journal_entries
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.140 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_literacy
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.110 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_colonial_integrity
		trigger = {
			any_state_region = {
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = root }
				any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } }
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = { not = { this = root is_country_type = decentralized } } }
			}
		}
		every_state_region = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = root }
				any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } }
				any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no owner = { not = { this = root is_country_type = decentralized } } }
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = { is_incorporated = no owner = { not = { this = root is_country_type = decentralized } } }
				set_state_owner = root
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_institutions#机构
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.121 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_war_support#战争支持度
		if = { limit = { any_scope_war = { count > 0 } } set_variable = daoyu_root_war_support hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.120 popup = yes } } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = at_peace_nocontext_tt hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_political_movements#政治运动
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.150 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_interest_groups#利益集团
		set_global_variable = daoyu_from_common
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#常用
daoyu.108 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = PRESTIGE#威望
	flavor = daoyu_current_prestige
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional }
		first_valid = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } } desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_current_prestige }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 3
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } }
			if = { limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
		}
		else = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_country_prestige_var } } if = { limit = { is_ai = yes } set_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var months = 1 value = 0 } } else = { set_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var value = 0 } } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
	}
	option = {
		name = CLEAR_STATE
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_variable = daoyu_country_prestige_var }
	}
	option = {
		name = +500
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 500 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = +200
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 200 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = +100
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 100 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = +50
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 50 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = +20
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 20 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = +10
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 10 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = -10
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = 10 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = -20
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = -20 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = -50
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = -50 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = -100
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = -100 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = -200
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = -200 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = -500
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { change_variable = { name = daoyu_country_prestige_var add = -500 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		set_global_variable = daoyu_back
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } remove_global_variable = daoyu_from_common trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	after = { daoyu_country_prestige_effect = yes if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_back } remove_global_variable = daoyu_back } else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.108 popup = yes } } }
}

daoyu.109 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = mustard_gas
	desc = concept_generated_pollution
	flavor = good_pollution_modifier
	event_image = { video = "middleeast_battlefield_trenches" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	duration = 3
	option = {
		name = good_pollution_modifier
		default_option = yes
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_modifier = mustard_gas } remove_modifier = mustard_gas remove_modifier = mustard_gas }
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		set_variable = { name = daoyu_no_mustard_gas years = 2 }
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_level_3
		effect_starting_pop_literacy_high = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_level_4
		effect_starting_pop_literacy_very_high = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_level_5
		every_scope_pop = { set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = { value = 0.8 if = { limit = { state = { is_incorporated = no } } multiply = 0.5 } } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_level_6
		every_scope_pop = { set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = { value = 1 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#战争中
daoyu.120 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_war_support#战争支持度
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_root_war_support } desc = daoyu_root_get_name }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_root_war_support } exists = scope:daoyu_target_country } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional }
		}
	}
	event_image = { video = "southamerica_war_civilians" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/american_civil_war"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_newspaper.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_root_war_support } } random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } not = { has_variable = daoyu_declare_war_initiator } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
	option = {
		name = SINGLE_GOODS_OR_EMPLOYMENT_MORE
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_root_war_support } every_scope_war = { add_war_war_support = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = 20 } } }
		else_if = { limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_war = { add_war_war_support = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = 20 } } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.120 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = SINGLE_GOODS_OR_EMPLOYMENT_LESS
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_root_war_support } every_scope_war = { add_war_war_support = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = -20 } } }
		else_if = { limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_war = { add_war_war_support = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = -20 } } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.120 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_root_war_support } remove_variable = daoyu_root_war_support hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } } }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.370 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } } }
	}
}

daoyu.130 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_power_bloc
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_dlc_feature = power_bloc_features } } desc = daoyu_no_dlc_create_power_bloc } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_dlc_feature = power_bloc_features is_in_power_bloc = no } desc = daoyu_no_power_bloc } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_dlc_feature = power_bloc_features exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } } desc = daoyu_target_country_power_bloc } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_dlc_feature = power_bloc_features is_power_bloc_leader = yes } desc = daoyu_root_power_bloc } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_dlc_feature = power_bloc_features is_in_power_bloc = no is_country_type = unrecognized } desc = concept_unrecognized_power } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_dlc_feature = power_bloc_features is_in_power_bloc = yes is_power_bloc_leader = no } desc = concept_power_bloc_member_non_leader } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_root_join_target_country_power_bloc#加入国家集团
		trigger = { is_in_power_bloc = no exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } }
		join_power_bloc = scope:daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.130 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_join_root_power_bloc#加入国家集团
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_in_power_bloc = no } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { join_power_bloc = root }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.130 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_power_bloc_modifier#国家集团修正
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.131 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_power_bloc_leverage#影响
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes } } }
		power_bloc = { add_leverage = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country value = 100 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.130 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_power_bloc_cohesion#凝聚力
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes power_bloc = { current_cohesion_percentage < 1 } }
		power_bloc = { add_cohesion_percent = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.130 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ADD_NEW_PRINCIPLE#添加原则
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.132 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_principle#移除原则
		trigger = { is_power_bloc_leader = yes }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_principle
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.132 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions
		default_option = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN

daoyu.142 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_journal_entries
	flavor = daoyu_satisfy_some_journal_entries_activation_condition
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 999
	option = {
		name = je_corn_laws#谷物法
		trigger = { nor = { has_variable = daoyu_je_corn_laws has_variable = corn_laws_abolished has_journal_entry = je_corn_laws } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { ig:ig_landowners = { is_marginal = yes } } ig:ig_landowners = { add_modifier = { name = daoyu_interest_group_approval multiplier = 1000 months = 1 } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str multiplier = 1000 months = 1 } } }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_export_priority_tariffs = g:grain } } set_tariffs_export_priority = g:grain }
			if = { limit = { ig:ig_landowners = { is_in_government = no } } ig:ig_landowners = { add_ruling_interest_group = yes } }
			if = { limit = { nor = { has_law = law_type:law_isolationism has_law = law_type:law_mercantilism } } activate_law = law_type:law_mercantilism }
			if = {
				limit = { not = { market_capital.market = { mg:grain = { market_goods_pricier > 0.25 } } } }
				every_market = { limit = { daoyu_can_create_trade_route_trigger = { SCOPE = root } } owner = { create_trade_route = { goods = grain level = 100 direction = import target = root.market } } }
			}
			set_variable = daoyu_je_corn_laws
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.142 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = je_corn_laws#谷物法
		trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_je_corn_laws has_journal_entry = je_corn_laws }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = daoyu_je_corn_laws has_journal_entry = je_corn_laws }
				activate_law = law_type:law_free_trade
				remove_variable = daoyu_je_corn_laws
			}
		}
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_unpause_the_game_and_wait_for_journal_entries_to_pop_up
		trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_je_corn_laws not = { has_journal_entry = je_corn_laws } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.142 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.140 popup = yes } }
	}
}

		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }

	duration = 0

		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country

			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } }
			if = { limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
		}
		else = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_approval_loyal#忠诚
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_interest_group = { hidden_effect = { remove_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_interest_group_approval multiplier = 40 months = -1 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_approval_angry#愤怒
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_interest_group = { hidden_effect = { remove_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_interest_group_approval multiplier = -40 months = -1 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.180 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = interest_group_approval_add#利益集团支持度
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.181 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_interest_group_political_strength#利益集团政治力量
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.181 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_ideologies#意识形态
		set_global_variable = daoyu_IG_ideologies
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.181 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TRIGGER_IS_IN_GOVERNMENT#加入政府
		set_global_variable = daoyu_add_ruling_interest_group
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.181 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TRIGGER_IS_IN_GOVERNMENT_NOT#从政府移除
		set_global_variable = daoyu_remove_ruling_interest_group
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.181 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_common } remove_global_variable = daoyu_from_common trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}

				if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_ig_intelligentsia_pol_str } } set_variable = { name = daoyu_ig_intelligentsia_pol_str value = 0 } }

				if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_ig_rural_folk_pol_str } } set_variable = { name = daoyu_ig_rural_folk_pol_str years = 1 value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}

					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_armed_forces_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_landowners_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_devout_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_industrialists_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_intelligentsia_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_petty_bourgeoisie_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_trade_unions_pol_str
					remove_variable = daoyu_ig_rural_folk_pol_str

			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.182 popup = yes } }
		}
	}

		name = NEXT_PAGE#下一页

		daoyu_determine_page_next = yes

#国家修正
daoyu.190 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_country_modifiers
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_country_desc }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		if = {
			limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
			random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.190 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.190 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country#调整目标国家
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.191 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_our_country#调整本国
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_target_country days = 1 } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.191 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_all_country_remove_all_modifiers
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } daoyu_has_country_modifiers_trigger = yes } }
		every_country = { daoyu_remove_all_country_modifier_effect = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.190 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_remove_all_modifiers
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country daoyu_has_country_modifiers_trigger = yes } }
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes daoyu_target_country daoyu_has_country_modifiers_trigger = yes } daoyu_remove_all_country_modifier_effect = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.190 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_root_remove_all_modifiers
		trigger = { daoyu_has_country_modifiers_trigger = yes }
		daoyu_remove_all_country_modifier_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.190 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.100 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.200 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_characters
	flavor = daoyu_cheat

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { ruler  = { ideology = { save_scope_as = daoyu_ruler_ideology } } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_country_agitator_slots_add#鼓动者槽位
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.201 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = daoyu_manage_character#管理角色

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_manage_character#管理角色
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } set_variable = daoyu_target_country } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
			else = { custom_tooltip = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_character#创建角色
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_create_character#创建角色
		custom_tooltip = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } set_variable = daoyu_target_country }  trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
			else = { custom_tooltip = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_royalist#保皇主义者

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_republican_leader#共和主义者
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 }
			root = { or = { has_law = law_type:law_presidential_republic has_law = law_type:law_parliamentary_republic } }
			any_scope_character = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader } }
		}
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader } } set_ideology = ideology:ideology_republican_leader }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ideology_theocrat#神权政治主义者
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_210 } has_law = law_type:law_theocracy any_scope_character = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat } } }
		every_scope_character = { limit = { not = { has_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat } } set_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat }

	}
	option = {

	}

		name = CHARACTER_HISTORICAL_HEADER#历史角色
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.290 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = RESIGN

	}

daoyu.210 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_manage_character
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_country_desc }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_negative_traits#负面特质
		trigger = {
			any_scope_character = {
				or = {
					has_trait = alcoholic
					has_trait = opium_addiction
					has_trait = cocaine_addiction
					has_trait = cancer
					has_trait = grifter
					has_trait = scarred
					has_trait = senile
					has_trait = syphilis
					has_trait = shellshocked
					has_trait = wounded
					has_trait = psychological_affliction
					has_trait = expensive_tastes
					has_trait = kidney_stones
					has_trait = beetle_ear
					has_trait = war_criminal
					has_trait = sickly
					has_trait = inept
					has_trait = inexperienced
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = arrogant }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = bigoted }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = imperious }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = reserved }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = cruel }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = hedonist }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = ruthless }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = bandit }
					and = { has_role = executive has_trait = political_appointee }
				}
			}
		}
		every_scope_character = {
			if = { limit = { has_trait = alcoholic } remove_trait = alcoholic }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = opium_addiction } remove_trait = opium_addiction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cocaine_addiction } remove_trait = cocaine_addiction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cancer } remove_trait = cancer }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = grifter } remove_trait = grifter }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = scarred } remove_trait = scarred }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = senile } remove_trait = senile }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = syphilis } remove_trait = syphilis }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = shellshocked } remove_trait = shellshocked }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = wounded } remove_trait = wounded }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = psychological_affliction } remove_trait = psychological_affliction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = expensive_tastes } remove_trait = expensive_tastes }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = kidney_stones } remove_trait = kidney_stones }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = beetle_ear } remove_trait = beetle_ear }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = war_criminal } remove_trait = war_criminal }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = sickly } remove_trait = sickly }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inept } remove_trait = inept }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inexperienced } remove_trait = inexperienced }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = arrogant } remove_trait = arrogant }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = bigoted } remove_trait = bigoted }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = imperious } remove_trait = imperious }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = reserved } remove_trait = reserved }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = cruel } remove_trait = cruel }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = hedonist } remove_trait = hedonist }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = ruthless } remove_trait = ruthless }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = bandit } remove_trait = bandit }
			if = { limit = { has_role = executive has_trait = political_appointee } remove_trait = political_appointee }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_our_country
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country has_variable = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } } }

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes } }
	}

		}
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.211 popup = yes } }
	}

daoyu.220 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_manage_character
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country any_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } } } desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = concept_culture } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country any_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } } } desc = daoyu_target_character_get_culture } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } desc = daoyu_mark_target_culture_get_name } }
	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_filter_army } remove_global_variable = daoyu_filter_army }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet } remove_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet }
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	option = {
		name = SET_CHARACTER_AS_RULER#成为统治者
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { is_ruler = no not = { has_role = executive } has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_set_character_as_ruler
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.222 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_executive_traits#经理特质
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = executive has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = {
			if = { limit = { has_trait = alcoholic } remove_trait = alcoholic }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = opium_addiction } remove_trait = opium_addiction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cocaine_addiction } remove_trait = cocaine_addiction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cancer } remove_trait = cancer }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = grifter } remove_trait = grifter }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = scarred } remove_trait = scarred }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = senile } remove_trait = senile }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = syphilis } remove_trait = syphilis }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = shellshocked } remove_trait = shellshocked }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = wounded } remove_trait = wounded }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = psychological_affliction } remove_trait = psychological_affliction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = expensive_tastes } remove_trait = expensive_tastes }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = kidney_stones } remove_trait = kidney_stones }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = beetle_ear } remove_trait = beetle_ear }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = war_criminal } remove_trait = war_criminal }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = sickly } remove_trait = sickly }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inept } remove_trait = inept }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inexperienced } remove_trait = inexperienced }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = arrogant } remove_trait = arrogant }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = bigoted } remove_trait = bigoted }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = imperious } remove_trait = imperious }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = reserved } remove_trait = reserved }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cruel } remove_trait = cruel }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = hedonist } remove_trait = hedonist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = ruthless } remove_trait = ruthless }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = bandit } remove_trait = bandit }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = political_appointee } remove_trait = political_appointee }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_entrepreneur } remove_trait = basic_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_entrepreneur } remove_trait = experienced_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_trait = expert_entrepreneur } } add_trait = expert_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_trait = daoyu_entrepreneur } } add_trait = daoyu_entrepreneur }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_character_change_culture#标记文化
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character or = { not = { has_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } not = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } } }
		if = { limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } scope:daoyu_target_character = { change_character_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { set_global_variable = daoyu_target_character_mark_target_culture set_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_begin trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_character_culture_save_mark_target_culture#标记文化
		#trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character or = { not = { has_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } not = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character.culture = { save_scope_as = daoyu_mark_target_culture }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { remove_trait = daoyu_target_character }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions
		remove_variable = daoyu_target_country
		set_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_exile#流放
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = agitator has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_exile_character
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.222 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_life_experience#人生经验
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_experience = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod#强迫信仰
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.230 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_character_traits#角色特质
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.240 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_ideology#意识形态
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.250 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = assassination_events.5.t#刺杀
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.260 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = character_health_add#角色健康
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_character_health_add
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.221 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = interest_group_approval_add#利益集团支持度
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.221 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_interest_group_political_strength#利益集团政治力量
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.221 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_change_interest_group#变更利益集团
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.229 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_ig_modifiers#删除利益集团所有修正
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character }
			or = {
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country any_interest_group = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval } } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country any_interest_group = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } } }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country }
			every_interest_group = {
				if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_approval } if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval } remove_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval } }
				if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } remove_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation#分配到其他编队
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = general has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_filter_army set_variable = daoyu_page_01
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.1 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation#分配到其他编队
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = admiral has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_filter_fleet set_variable = daoyu_page_01
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.1 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PROMOTE_COMMANDER#晋升
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { or = { has_role = general has_role = admiral } has_trait = daoyu_target_character commander_rank < 5 is_ruler = no } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_commander_rank = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { remove_trait = daoyu_target_character }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions
		remove_variable = daoyu_target_country 
		default_option = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } remove_trait = daoyu_target_character }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.210 popup = yes }
		}
		default_option = yes
	}
}

	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_character_as_ruler } } desc = SET_CHARACTER_AS_RULER }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_exile_character } } desc = oncept_exile }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_set_character_as_ruler exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { set_character_as_ruler = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_exile_character exists = scope:daoyu_target_character scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { exile_character = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_set_character_as_ruler
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_exile_character
		trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes }
	}
}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		random_character = {
			limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character }
			save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character
			if = { limit = { has_trait = traditionalist_commander } remove_trait = traditionalist_commander add_trait = celebrity_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = popular_commander } remove_trait = popular_commander add_trait = celebrity_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = stalwart_defender } remove_trait = stalwart_defender add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = trench_rat } remove_trait = trench_rat add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_artillery_commander } remove_trait = basic_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_artillery_commander } remove_trait = experienced_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_offensive_planner } remove_trait = basic_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_offensive_planner }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_offensive_planner } remove_trait = experienced_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_offensive_planner }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_defensive_strategist } remove_trait = basic_defensive_strategist add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist } remove_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_naval_commander } remove_trait = basic_naval_commander add_trait = expert_naval_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_naval_commander } remove_trait = experienced_naval_commander add_trait = expert_naval_commander }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = convoy_raider_commander } remove_trait = convoy_raider_commander add_trait = expert_convoy_raider }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_convoy_raider } remove_trait = experienced_convoy_raider add_trait = expert_convoy_raider }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_diplomat } remove_trait = basic_diplomat add_trait = masterful_diplomat }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_diplomat } remove_trait = experienced_diplomat add_trait = masterful_diplomat }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_colonial_administrator } remove_trait = basic_colonial_administrator add_trait = expert_colonial_administrator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_colonial_administrator } remove_trait = experienced_colonial_administrator add_trait = expert_colonial_administrator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_political_operator } remove_trait = basic_political_operator add_trait = expert_political_operator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_political_operator } remove_trait = experienced_political_operator add_trait = expert_political_operator }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inspirational_orator } remove_trait = inspirational_orator add_trait = firebrand }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_entrepreneur } remove_trait = basic_entrepreneur add_trait = expert_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_entrepreneur } remove_trait = experienced_entrepreneur add_trait = expert_entrepreneur }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ACHIEVEMENT_FILTER_BUTTON_ALL
		scope:daoyu_target_character = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = yes is_heir = yes }
				add_trait = traditionalist_commander add_trait = expert_political_operator add_trait = expert_colonial_administrator add_trait = firebrand
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = general }
				add_trait = pillager add_trait = surveyor add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist add_trait = resupply_commander add_trait = forest_commander add_trait = plains_commander
				add_trait = mountain_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
				add_trait = traditionalist_commander
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = admiral }
				add_trait = expert_naval_commander add_trait = expert_convoy_raider add_trait = dockyard_master add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
				add_trait = traditionalist_commander
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = politician }
				add_trait = expert_political_operator add_trait = firebrand add_trait = literary
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_role = agitator }
				add_trait = expert_political_operator add_trait = firebrand add_trait = erudite add_trait = engineer add_trait = literary
			}
			add_trait = explorer add_trait = erudite add_trait = engineer add_trait = master_bureaucrat add_trait = celebrity_commander add_trait = masterful_diplomat add_trait = expert_entrepreneur
		}
	}
	option = { name = explorer trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = explorer } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = explorer } }
	option = { name = erudite trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = erudite } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = erudite } }
	option = { name = engineer trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = engineer } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = engineer } }
	option = { name = master_bureaucrat trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = master_bureaucrat } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = master_bureaucrat } }
	option = { name = literary trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { is_commander = no not = { has_trait = literary } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = literary } }
	option = { name = masterful_diplomat trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = masterful_diplomat } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = masterful_diplomat } }
	option = { name = celebrity_commander trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { not = { has_trait = celebrity_commander } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = celebrity_commander } }
	option = { name = pillager trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = general not = { has_trait = pillager } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = pillager } }
	option = { name = surveyor trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { has_role = general not = { has_trait = surveyor } } } scope:daoyu_target_character = { add_trait = surveyor } }

		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { or = { has_role = agitator interest_group = { or = { is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions } } } not = { has_trait = social_bandit } } }

#添加人物修正
daoyu.245 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_health_add } desc = character_health_add }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_health_add } or = { any_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character has_role = general } has_variable = daoyu_generals_orders } } desc = daoyu_general_modifier }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_health_add } or = { any_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character has_role = admiral } has_variable = daoyu_admirals_orders } } desc = daoyu_admiral_modifier }
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { nor = { has_variable = daoyu_generals_orders has_variable = daoyu_admirals_orders } exists = scope:daoyu_target_character } desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_generals_orders } desc = concept_generals } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_admirals_orders } desc = concept_admirals } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_health_add } random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character remove_modifier = daoyu_negative_character_health_add remove_modifier = daoyu_character_health_add } }
		else = { random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character remove_modifier =  remove_modifier =  remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier remove_modifier = daoyu_admiral_modifier } }
	}
	option = { name = 1x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 1 } }
	option = { name = 2x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 2 } }
	option = { name = 5x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 5 } }
	option = { name = 10x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 10 } }
	option = { name = 15x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 15 } }
	option = { name = 20x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 20 } }
	option = { name = 25x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 25 } }
	option = { name = 50x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 50 } }
	option = { name = 100x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 100 } }
	option = { name = 200x daoyu_add_military_modifier = { MULTIPLIER = 200 } }
	option = {
		name = CANCEL
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_character_health_add
		if = { limit = { or = { has_variable = daoyu_generals_orders has_variable = daoyu_admirals_orders } } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.240 popup = yes } }
	}

	}

#杀死角色
daoyu.260 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = assassination_events.5.t
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country any_character = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } } } desc = daoyu_target_character_get_name } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "southamerica_public_figure_assassination" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_skull.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_character }
	}
	option = {
		name = assassination_events.8.a
		hidden_effect = { scope:daoyu_target_character = { remove_trait = daoyu_target_character } }
		scope:daoyu_target_character = { kill_character = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = assassination_events.6.a
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#角色
daoyu.270 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_create_character
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_create_character_gender }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male } desc = CHARACTER_MALE }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_female } desc = CHARACTER_FEMALE }
		}
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_country_desc }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = { limit = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male has_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_female } } set_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male }
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = CHARACTER_MALE#创建角色性别
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_female
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CHARACTER_FEMALE#创建角色性别
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_female
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_our_country
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } } }
		remove_variable = daoyu_target_country
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } set_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_politician#创建政治家
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_politician
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_agitator#创建鼓动者
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_agitator
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_ruler#创建统治者
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_ruler
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_heir#继任者
		trigger = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country coa_monarchy_trigger = yes } }
		if = { limit = { any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country ruler = { age < 18 } } } custom_tooltip = daoyu_too_low_age hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_last_name_random set_global_variable = daoyu_create_heir hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_general#创建陆军将领
		trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country has_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_general
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_admiral#创建海军将领
		trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country has_global_variable = daoyu_create_character_male }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.200 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#选择利益集团
daoyu.271 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_create_character
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } } desc = daoyu_target_country } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_general has_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } desc = daoyu_mf_1 } }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_general } desc = ai_goal_recruit_generals }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } desc = ai_goal_recruit_admirals }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_politician } desc = concept_politician }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_agitator } desc = concept_agitator }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_ruler } desc = concept_ruler }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_heir } desc = concept_heir }
		}
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		remove_variable = daoyu_ig_armed_forces remove_variable = daoyu_ig_devout remove_variable = daoyu_ig_industrialists remove_variable = daoyu_ig_intelligentsia
		remove_variable = daoyu_ig_landowners remove_variable = daoyu_ig_petty_bourgeoisie remove_variable = daoyu_ig_rural_folk remove_variable = daoyu_ig_trade_unions
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_armed_forces
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_armed_forces" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_devout
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_devout" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_industrialists
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_industrialists" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_intelligentsia
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_intelligentsia" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_landowners
		set_global_variable = daoyu_noble daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_landowners" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_petty_bourgeoisie
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_petty_bourgeoisie" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_rural_folk
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_rural_folk" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ig_trade_unions
		daoyu_create_character = { IG = "ig_trade_unions" }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions } }
		set_variable = daoyu_return
		daoyu_remove_create_character_flag = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_general remove_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return } remove_variable = daoyu_return trigger_event = { id = daoyu.270 popup = yes } }
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_general has_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_character_interactions or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_create_general has_global_variable = daoyu_create_admiral } }
			if = { random_scope_character = { limit = { has_trait = daoyu_target_character } transfer_to_formation = scope:daoyu_mf_1 } }
			daoyu_remove_create_character_flag = yes
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes }
		}
		else = { daoyu_remove_create_character_flag = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#批量管理角色
daoyu.280 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_generals_orders } desc = daoyu_generals_orders }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_admirals_orders } desc = daoyu_admirals_orders }
		}
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_skill_traits
		trigger = {
			has_variable = daoyu_generals_orders
			any_country = {
				has_variable = daoyu_target_country 
				any_scope_general = {
					is_ruler = no
					not = {
						has_trait = pillager has_trait = surveyor has_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist has_trait = resupply_commander has_trait = forest_commander has_trait = plains_commander has_trait = explorer
						has_trait = mountain_commander has_trait = expert_artillery_commander has_trait = expert_offensive_planner has_trait = expert_defensive_strategist
					}
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_scope_general = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_trait = trench_rat remove_trait = basic_artillery_commander remove_trait = experienced_artillery_commander remove_trait = experienced_defensive_strategist
					remove_trait = basic_offensive_planner remove_trait = experienced_offensive_planner remove_trait = basic_defensive_strategist remove_trait = stalwart_defender
				}
				add_trait = pillager add_trait = surveyor add_trait = defense_in_depth_specialist add_trait = resupply_commander add_trait = forest_commander add_trait = plains_commander add_trait = explorer
				add_trait = mountain_commander add_trait = expert_artillery_commander add_trait = expert_offensive_planner add_trait = expert_defensive_strategist set_variable = daoyu_betrayal_will_die
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_skill_traits
		trigger = {
			has_variable = daoyu_admirals_orders
			any_country = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country any_scope_admiral = { is_ruler = no not = { has_trait = dockyard_master has_trait = expert_naval_commander has_trait = expert_convoy_raider has_trait = explorer } } }
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_scope_admiral = {
				limit = { is_ruler = no }
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_trait = basic_naval_commander remove_trait = experienced_naval_commander remove_trait = convoy_raider_commander remove_trait = experienced_convoy_raider
				}
				add_trait = dockyard_master add_trait = expert_naval_commander add_trait = expert_convoy_raider add_trait = explorer
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.280 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = daoyu_personality_traits
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.281 popup = yes } }
	}

			if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 2 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 2 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 3 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 3 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 4 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 4 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
			else_if = { limit = { any_scope_general = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 5 } } every_scope_general = { limit = { is_ruler = no commander_rank < 5 } add_commander_rank = 1 } }
		}

	}

	duration = 0

		name = ethiopia.1.t#法外王侯
