		custom_tooltip = concept_ruler
		create_character = {
			first_name = Tewodros last_name = Solomon historical = yes ruler = yes noble = yes age = 45 dna = dna_emperor_tewodros_02 interest_group = ig_landowners culture = cu:amhara
			religion = rel:oriental_orthodox ideology = ideology_royalist traits = { romantic expert_offensive_planner } on_created = { add_modifier = { name = tewodros_modifier } }
		}
		set_global_variable = tewodros_var
	}
	option = {
		name = ethiopia.1.t#法外王侯
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = tewodros_var } }
		custom_tooltip = concept_party_leader

			first_name = Tewodros last_name = Solomon historical = yes noble = yes age = 45 dna = dna_emperor_tewodros_02 interest_group = ig_landowners culture = cu:amhara
			religion = rel:oriental_orthodox ideology = ideology_royalist traits = { romantic expert_offensive_planner } on_created = { add_modifier = { name = tewodros_modifier } }
		}
		set_global_variable = tewodros_var
	}
	option = {
		name = Marx#马克思
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = marx_happened } }
		if = { limit = { empty_agitator_slots = 0 } custom_tooltip = NO_AVAILABLE_AGITATOR_SLOTS }
		else_if = { limit = { game_date < 1818.5.5 } custom_tooltip = daoyu_was_born_on custom_tooltip = 1818.5.5 }
		else_if = { limit = { game_date < 1836.1.1 } custom_tooltip = trait_child_desc }
		else_if = {
			set_variable = daoyu_return set_global_variable = marx_happened
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = rationalism } } add_technology_researched = rationalism }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = academia } } add_technology_researched = academia }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = democracy } } add_technology_researched = democracy }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = empiricism } } add_technology_researched = empiricism }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = mass_communication } } add_technology_researched = mass_communication }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = dialectics } } add_technology_researched = dialectics }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = egalitarianism } } add_technology_researched = egalitarianism }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_technology_researched = labor_movement } } add_technology_researched = labor_movement }

		}

		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID } }

			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality }

			random_state = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } save_scope_as = daoyu_high_growth_mortality_state }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } } }

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}

		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_target_country#失业人口送目标国家
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_variable = daoyu_high_growth_mortality } } any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_country.capital } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.302 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_high_growth_mortality#失业人口送目标国家

				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { is_country_type = decentralized }
				aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
				not = { is_subject_of = root }
			}
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = { target_country = scope:daoyu_target_country war = yes type = dp_make_puppet }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_diplomatic_play_annex_war_against_target_country_war_now#吞并国家
		trigger = {
			aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			not = { is_country_type = decentralized is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { is_country_type = decentralized is_subject_of = root }
				aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			}
		}
		create_diplomatic_play = { target_country = scope:daoyu_target_country war = yes type = dp_annex_war }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.330 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_diplomatic_actions
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_330
	}
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_join_us_in_the_war#参战
		trigger = {
			aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
			not = { is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				has_modifier = daoyu_target_country is_at_war = no
				aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes
				not = { is_subject_of = root has_war_with = root }
				any_scope_state = { any_neighbouring_state = { owner = { has_war_with = root } } }
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { violate_sovereignty_join = { violator = root target = scope:daoyu_target_country join_violator = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = low_liberty_desire#低独立倾向
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes is_subject = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country liberty_desire > 5 } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { add_liberty_desire = -100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_high_liberty_desire#高独立倾向
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes is_subject = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country liberty_desire < 95 } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { add_liberty_desire = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = increase_relations#改善关系
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country relations:root < 100 not = { is_country_type = decentralized } } }
		change_relations = { country = scope:daoyu_target_country value = 20 }
	}
	option = {
		name = damage_relations#破坏关系
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country relations:root > -100 not = { is_country_type = decentralized } } }
		change_relations = { country = scope:daoyu_target_country value = -20 }
	}
	option = {
		name = revolution_pulse_events.13.t#无偿援助
		trigger = { gold_reserves > 1000 scope:daoyu_target_country = { gold_reserves < gold_reserves_limit } }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_330
		set_global_variable = daoyu_339
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_rank#国际地位
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country is_country_type = unrecognized } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_country_type = recognized }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_rank#国际地位
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country is_country_type = decentralized } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_country_type = unrecognized }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_truce#停战协议
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { is_country_type = decentralized } } not = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_truce_with = root } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { create_unidirectional_truce = { country = root months = 60 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_end_truce_root_between_target_country#移除停战协议
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } or = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_truce_with = root } has_truce_with = scope:daoyu_target_country } }
		end_truce = scope:daoyu_target_country
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_end_truce_all_between_target_country#移除停战协议
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } any_country = { is_ai = yes or = { has_truce_with = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_truce_with = prev } } } }
		every_country = { limit = { has_truce_with = scope:daoyu_target_country } end_truce = scope:daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_defensive_pact#共同防御条约
		trigger = {
			aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes has_diplomatic_relevance = scope:daoyu_target_country
			not = { is_subject_of = root has_war_with = root is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country has_diplomatic_pact = { type = defensive_pact who = scope:daoyu_target_country } }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { is_country_type = decentralized } aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes not = { is_subject_of = root has_war_with = root } }

			scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { is_country_type = decentralized } aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes not = { is_subject_of = root has_war_with = root } }

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.330 popup = yes } }

		name = RESIGN

	}

daoyu.340 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_state_options
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cede_state_to_target_country#赠予他国地区
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.341 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cede_target_country_state#他国割让地区
		trigger = { any_country = { any_scope_state = { count > 1 } has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { is_sea_adjacent = yes count = 1 } } every_scope_state = { limit = { is_sea_adjacent = no } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			else = { every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.345 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_claim_target_country_state#宣称他国地区
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { not = { has_claim_by = root } } } }
		random_country = {
			limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { not = { has_claim_by = root } } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.347 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_claim#宣称目标国家全部领土
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { not = { has_claim_by = root } } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { limit = { not = { has_claim_by = root } } state_region = { add_claim = root } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_claim_1#放弃对目标国领土的宣称
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { has_claim_by = root } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_claim_by = root } state_region = { remove_claim = root } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_claim_2#目标国放弃对我国领土的宣称
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } any_scope_state = { has_claim_by = scope:daoyu_target_country } }

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_claim_2#目标国放弃对我国领土的宣称
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } any_scope_state = { has_claim_by = scope:daoyu_target_country } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_claim_by = scope:daoyu_target_country } state_region = { remove_claim = scope:daoyu_target_country } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporate_state#整合地区
		if = {
			limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { is_treaty_port = no is_incorporated = no state_region = { not = { any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } } } } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
				every_scope_state = { limit = { is_treaty_port = no is_incorporated = no state_region = { not = { any_scope_state = { owner = { is_country_type = decentralized } } } } } set_state_type = incorporated }
			}
		}
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_target_country_get_name custom_tooltip = concept_incorporated_states }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#赠予他国地区
daoyu.341 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_cede_state_to_target_country
	flavor = { first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } } }
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } } }
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
			or = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.341 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
			any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		}
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_cede_state set_state_owner = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.341 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_states
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } remove_variable = daoyu_cede_state set_state_type = incorporated } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unincorporated_states
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } remove_variable = daoyu_cede_state } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_cede_state } } } }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.340 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_agricultural_expansion#投资农业
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_agricultural_expansion } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_agricultural_expansion }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_resource_expansion#扩大资源产业
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_resource_expansion } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_resource_expansion }
	}

		name = ai_strategy_industrial_expansion#工业化
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_industrial_expansion } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_industrial_expansion }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_colonial_extraction#殖民地开采
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_colonial_extraction } is_subject = yes is_country_type = colonial } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_colonial_extraction }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_plantation_economy#种植园经济
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_plantation_economy }
				or = {
					capital.region = sr:region_dixie
					country_is_in_south_america = yes
					country_is_in_central_america = yes
					country_is_in_india = yes
					country_is_in_southeast_asia = yes
					country_is_in_africa = yes
					country_is_in_east_asia = yes
					country_is_in_middle_east = yes
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_plantation_economy }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_placate_population#安抚群众
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_placate_population } has_law = law_type:law_traditionalism } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_placate_population }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.350 popup = yes } }
}

		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { liberty_desire > 50 } } custom_tooltip = daoyu_high_liberty_desire }
		else_if = { limit = { is_diplomatic_play_enemy_of = overlord } custom_tooltip = daoyu_is_diplomatic_play_enemy_of_overlord }
		else = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_subject_overlord_compliance } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.350 popup = yes } }
}

			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country has_strategy = ai_strategy_conservative_agenda } } desc = ai_strategy_conservative_agenda }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country has_strategy = ai_strategy_reactionary_agenda } } desc = ai_strategy_reactionary_agenda }

			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country has_strategy = ai_strategy_nationalist_agenda } } desc = ai_strategy_nationalist_agenda }

		}
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_conservative_agenda#保守派目标
		trigger = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_conservative_agenda } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_conservative_agenda }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_reactionary_agenda#弘扬传统价值
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_reactionary_agenda }
				exists = ruler
				ruler = {
					interest_group = {
						nor = {
							is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
							is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
							is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
						}
					}
					or = {
						has_ideology = ideology:ideology_traditionalist
						has_ideology = ideology:ideology_slaver
						has_ideology = ideology:ideology_theocrat
					}
				}
				or = {
					and = { exists = ig:ig_landowners ig:ig_landowners = { is_marginal = no } }
					and = { exists = ig:ig_devout ig:ig_devout = { is_marginal = no } }
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_reactionary_agenda }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_progressive_agenda#促进自由派改革
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_progressive_agenda }
				or = {
					and = { exists = ig:ig_intelligentsia ig:ig_intelligentsia = { is_marginal = no } }
					and = { exists = ig:ig_industrialists ig:ig_industrialists = { is_marginal = no } }
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_progressive_agenda }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_egalitarian_agenda#增进平等
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_egalitarian_agenda }
				has_technology_researched = egalitarianism
				exists = ig:ig_trade_unions
				ig:ig_trade_unions = { is_marginal = no }
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_egalitarian_agenda }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_nationalist_agenda#强化民族国家
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_nationalist_agenda }
				has_technology_researched = nationalism
				or = {
					and = { exists = ig:ig_armed_forces ig:ig_armed_forces = { is_marginal = no } }
					and = { exists = ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { is_marginal = no } }
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_nationalist_agenda }
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_strategy_maintain_mandate_of_heaven#维系天命
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country
				not = { has_strategy = ai_strategy_maintain_mandate_of_heaven }
				exists = c:CHI
				this = c:CHI
				is_country_type = unrecognized
				has_law = law_type:law_monarchy
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_strategy = ai_strategy_maintain_mandate_of_heaven }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	after = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.350 popup = yes } }
}

daoyu.360 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_political_lobbies
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } desc = daoyu_root_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } desc = NONE } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } desc = concept_political_lobbies_short } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { this = root } any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { this = root } any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } } desc = NONE } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { this = root } any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } } desc = concept_political_lobbies_short } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { or = { not = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { this = root } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.360 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = lobby_category_domestic#国内游说团
		trigger = { any_political_lobby = { count > 0 } }
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		if = { limit = { any_political_lobby = { count = 1 } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { any_political_lobby = { count > 1 } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.361 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_get_name#目标国家
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { this = root } any_political_lobby = { count > 0 } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_political_lobby = { count = 1 } } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } } }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.361 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes }
	}
}

daoyu.361 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name
	flavor = concept_political_lobbies
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			random_political_lobby = { save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_1 }
			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_2 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_2 }
			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_3 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_3 }
			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_4 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_4 }
			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_5 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_5 }

			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_7 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_7 }
			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_8 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_8 }
			random_political_lobby = { limit = { daoyu_target_trigger_9 = { FLAG = tpl } } save_scope_as = daoyu_tpl_9 }
		}
	}
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_1 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_1 } scope:daoyu_tpl_1 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_2 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_2 scope:daoyu_tpl_2 = { daoyu_target_trigger_2 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_2 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_3 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_3 scope:daoyu_tpl_3 = { daoyu_target_trigger_3 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_3 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_4 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_4 scope:daoyu_tpl_4 = { daoyu_target_trigger_4 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_4 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_5 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_5 scope:daoyu_tpl_5 = { daoyu_target_trigger_5 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_5 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_6 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_6 scope:daoyu_tpl_6 = { daoyu_target_trigger_6 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_6 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_7 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_7 scope:daoyu_tpl_7 = { daoyu_target_trigger_7 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_7 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_8 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_8 scope:daoyu_tpl_8 = { daoyu_target_trigger_8 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_8 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	option = { name = daoyu_tpl_9 trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_tpl_9 scope:daoyu_tpl_9 = { daoyu_target_trigger_9 = { FLAG = tpl } } } scope:daoyu_tpl_9 = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }

		set_variable = daoyu_return
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }

			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return }
			remove_variable = daoyu_return

			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.360 popup = yes } }
		}
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } }
	}

#游说团
daoyu.362 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } desc = DISBAND_COMPANY } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { random_political_lobby = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_political_lobby } }
	}
	option = {
		name = appeasement_lobby_gain#游说团满意度提高
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } }
		scope:daoyu_target_political_lobby = { change_appeasement = { amount = 2 factor = catalyst_event_positive } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = appeasement_lobby_loss#游说团满意度降低
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } }
		scope:daoyu_target_political_lobby = { change_appeasement = { amount = -2 factor = catalyst_event_negative } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_lobby_member#任意利益集团加入游说团
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_interest_group = { is_member_of_any_lobby = no } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_add_lobby_member
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.363 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_lobby_member#任意利益集团离开游说团
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } scope:daoyu_target_political_lobby = { any_lobby_member = { count > 1 } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_remove_lobby_member
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.363 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = political_lobby_disbanded_notification_group#政治游说团解散
		trigger = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } }
		set_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded }
		remove_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { random_political_lobby = { limit = { this = scope:daoyu_target_political_lobby } disband_political_lobby = yes } }
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_political_lobby = { count > 0 } } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.361 popup = yes } } }
		else = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
			random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
			hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.360 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded } remove_variable = daoyu_political_lobby_disbanded trigger_event = { id = daoyu.362 popup = yes } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_political_lobby = { count = 0 } } } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.370 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.361 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}

		trigger = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions set_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war set_variable = daoyu_return
	}
	option = {
		name = dp_regime_change#政权更迭
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } exists = scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator = { not = { is_country_type = decentralized } aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes not = { is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_target_country } }
				scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { is_country_type = decentralized } not = { is_subject_of = scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator } }
			}
			scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator = { create_diplomatic_play = { name = regime_change target_country = scope:daoyu_target_country type = dp_regime_change } }
		}
		else = { custom_tooltip = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war set_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed
	}
	option = {
		name = dp_give_foreign_investment_rights#投资权
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } exists = scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator = { not = { can_create_diplomatic_pact = { target = scope:daoyu_target_country type = foreign_investment_rights } } } } custom_tooltip = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID }
		else = { scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator = { create_diplomatic_play = { name = humiliation target_country = scope:daoyu_target_country type = dp_give_foreign_investment_rights } } }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war set_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed
	}
	option = {
		name = dp_humiliation#羞辱
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } exists = scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = no } } custom_tooltip = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID }

	}
	option = {
		name = TRIGGER_IS_WAR#激化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed any_diplomatic_play = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } }
		random_diplomatic_play = { limit = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } add_escalation = 20 }
	}
	option = {
		name = TRIGGER_IS_WAR_NOT
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed any_diplomatic_play = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } }
		random_diplomatic_play = { limit = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } add_escalation = -20 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_join_diplomatic_play_initiator#加入
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_join_declare_war } any_diplomatic_play = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_join_declare_war
		random_diplomatic_play = { limit = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } add_initiator_backers = { root } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_join_diplomatic_play_target#加入
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_join_declare_war } any_diplomatic_play = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_join_declare_war
		random_diplomatic_play = { limit = { daoyu_declare_war_diplomatic_play = yes } add_target_backers = { root } }
	}
	option = {
		name = lobby_events.30.b#用外交行动平息他们的愤怒
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } exists = scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
		scope:daoyu_declare_war_initiator = { remove_variable = daoyu_declare_war_initiator } remove_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war set_variable = daoyu_return
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		trigger = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_declare_war_initiator } remove_variable = daoyu_declare_war_initiator add_modifier = { name = daoyu_target_country days = 1 } }
		set_variable = daoyu_return hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.370 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = QUIT
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } }
		set_variable = daoyu_return
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed } random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_declare_war_initiator } remove_variable = daoyu_declare_war_initiator } remove_global_variable = daoyu_declare_war_completed }
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_join_declare_war } remove_global_variable = daoyu_join_declare_war }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return } remove_variable = daoyu_return }
		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.375 popup = yes } } }
	}
}

		}
	}

daoyu.400 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = ECONOMY#经济
	flavor = daoyu_common_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_capitalists_meeting.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/capitalists_meeting"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_companies_add } } set_variable = { name = daoyu_companies_add value = 1 } }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_variable = daoyu_free_charters_add } } set_variable = { name = daoyu_free_charters_add value = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DISCOVERABLE_RESOURCES#可发现的资源
		trigger = {
			any_scope_state = {
				or = {
					has_potential_resource = bg_rubber
					has_potential_resource = bg_oil_extraction
					has_potential_resource = bg_banana_plantations
					has_potential_resource = bg_gold_mining
					has_potential_resource = bg_opium_plantations
					has_potential_resource = bg_tobacco_plantations
				}
			}
		}
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_potential_resource = bg_rubber } force_resource_discovery = bg_rubber }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_potential_resource = bg_oil_extraction } force_resource_discovery = bg_oil_extraction }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_potential_resource = bg_banana_plantations } force_resource_discovery = bg_banana_plantations }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_potential_resource = bg_gold_mining } force_resource_discovery = bg_gold_mining }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_potential_resource = bg_opium_plantations } force_resource_discovery = bg_opium_plantations }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_potential_resource = bg_tobacco_plantations } force_resource_discovery = bg_tobacco_plantations }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = state_expected_sol_mult#最低预期生活水平
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.402 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_country_monopoly#国家垄断
		trigger = { daoyu_can_country_monopolized_trigger = yes }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.410 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = country_max_companies_add#公司上限
		if = { limit = { exists = var:daoyu_companies_add } hidden_effect = { remove_modifier = daoyu_companies_add } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_companies_add multiplier = var:daoyu_companies_add months = -1 } }
		if = { limit = { exists = var:daoyu_companies_add } change_variable = { name = daoyu_companies_add add = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_free_charters_add#免费公司特许
		if = { limit = { exists = var:daoyu_free_charters_add } hidden_effect = { remove_modifier = daoyu_free_charters_add } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_free_charters_add multiplier = var:daoyu_free_charters_add months = -1 } }
		if = { limit = { exists = var:daoyu_free_charters_add } change_variable = { name = daoyu_free_charters_add add = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_company#解散公司
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu_company.1 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_executive_traits#经理特质
		trigger = {
			any_scope_character = {
				has_role = executive
				or = {
					has_trait = alcoholic
					has_trait = opium_addiction
					has_trait = cocaine_addiction
					has_trait = cancer
					has_trait = grifter
					has_trait = scarred
					has_trait = senile
					has_trait = syphilis
					has_trait = shellshocked
					has_trait = wounded
					has_trait = psychological_affliction
					has_trait = expensive_tastes
					has_trait = kidney_stones
					has_trait = beetle_ear
					has_trait = war_criminal
					has_trait = sickly
					has_trait = inept
					has_trait = inexperienced
					has_trait = arrogant
					has_trait = bigoted
					has_trait = imperious
					has_trait = reserved
					has_trait = cruel
					has_trait = hedonist
					has_trait = ruthless
					has_trait = bandit
					has_trait = political_appointee
					not = { has_trait = expert_entrepreneur }
					not = { has_trait = daoyu_entrepreneur }
				}
			}
		}
		every_scope_character = {
			limit = { has_role = executive }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = alcoholic } remove_trait = alcoholic }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = opium_addiction } remove_trait = opium_addiction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cocaine_addiction } remove_trait = cocaine_addiction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cancer } remove_trait = cancer }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = grifter } remove_trait = grifter }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = scarred } remove_trait = scarred }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = senile } remove_trait = senile }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = syphilis } remove_trait = syphilis }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = shellshocked } remove_trait = shellshocked }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = wounded } remove_trait = wounded }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = psychological_affliction } remove_trait = psychological_affliction }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = expensive_tastes } remove_trait = expensive_tastes }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = kidney_stones } remove_trait = kidney_stones }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = beetle_ear } remove_trait = beetle_ear }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = war_criminal } remove_trait = war_criminal }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = sickly } remove_trait = sickly }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inept } remove_trait = inept }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = inexperienced } remove_trait = inexperienced }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = arrogant } remove_trait = arrogant }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = bigoted } remove_trait = bigoted }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = imperious } remove_trait = imperious }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = reserved } remove_trait = reserved }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = cruel } remove_trait = cruel }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = hedonist } remove_trait = hedonist }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = ruthless } remove_trait = ruthless }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = bandit } remove_trait = bandit }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = political_appointee } remove_trait = political_appointee }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = basic_entrepreneur } remove_trait = basic_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { has_trait = experienced_entrepreneur } remove_trait = experienced_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_trait = expert_entrepreneur } } add_trait = expert_entrepreneur }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_trait = daoyu_entrepreneur } } add_trait = daoyu_entrepreneur }
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_market_price#市场价格
		set_global_variable = daoyu_market_price
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.580 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_banned#禁止某货物
		set_global_variable = daoyu_banned
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.580 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = pmg_ownership#所有制
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.440 popup = yes } }
	}

	}

		name = daoyu_unemployed_disappear#清理失业
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			daoyu_auto_unemployed_effcet = yes
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_money
		if = { limit = { gold_reserves = gold_reserves_limit } custom_tooltip = stockpiling_gold_alert_setting_name }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_3 } add_treasury = 1000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_4 } add_treasury = 10000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_5 } add_treasury = 100000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_6 } add_treasury = 1000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_7 } add_treasury = 10000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_8 } add_treasury = 100000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_9 } add_treasury = 1000000000 }

	option = {
		name = concept_investment_pool

		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_4 } add_investment_pool = 10000 }

		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_7 } add_investment_pool = 10000000 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_money_8 } add_investment_pool = 100000000 }

	option = {

#所有制
daoyu.440 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = pmg_ownership
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_country_desc }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		if = {
			limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
			random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.440 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#重新选目标
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.440 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_target_country#调整目标国家
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.441 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_modify_our_country#调整本国
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_target_country days = 1 } }
		save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.441 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.400 popup = yes } }
	}
}

#自给农提醒
daoyu.461 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = scope:daoyu_peasants_exhaustion
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion
	flavor = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_located
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 3
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state }
			remove_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state
			save_scope_as = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = bureaucracy.3.c
		default_option = yes
	}
}
daoyu.462 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week }
			set_variable = { name = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_week_on weeks = 1 }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.462 weeks = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants }
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } }
					if = { limit = { free_arable_land < 5 } state_region = { add_arable_land = 5 } }
					create_pop = { size = 2000 working_adult_ratio = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } not = { has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state } }
					set_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state
				}
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state }
					root = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.461 popup = yes } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
daoyu.463 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month }
			set_variable = { name = daoyu_peasants_exhaustion_month_on months = 1 }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.463 months = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = daoyu_auto_create_peasants }
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } }
					if = { limit = { free_arable_land < 5 } state_region = { add_arable_land = 5 } }
					create_pop = { size = 2000 working_adult_ratio = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } not = { has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state } }
					set_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state
				}
				every_scope_state = {
					limit = { not = { any_scope_pop = { is_pop_type = peasants } } has_variable = daoyu_has_peasants_state }

				}

		}
	}
}

		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
	}

		name = russification_modifier#民族同化

		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_root_get_name custom_tooltip = daoyu_state_not_eligible_mass_migration hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod#强迫信仰
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.520 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_mark_target_culture#标记文化
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
			else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_begin trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_obsession#痴迷

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.580 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect#一键洗地
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		set_global_variable = daoyu_500
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.590 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_solve_lag#低配置主机解决卡顿
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }

		name = RESIGN

daoyu.510 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu } desc = law_cultural_exclusion }#文化排斥
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu } desc = law_multicultural }#文化多元
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } desc = russification_modifier }#民族同化
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } } desc = daoyu_nul }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } desc = daoyu_country_has_primary_culture_more_than_one }
		}
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } } desc = daoyu_nul }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		}
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_root_get_name }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } } desc = daoyu_has_only_one }#只有一个
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } } desc = daoyu_has_over_one }#有多个
		}
		first_valid = { desc = concept_primary_culture }#主流文化
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count = 0 } } desc = daoyu_has_no }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count > 1 } } desc = daoyu_has }
		}
		first_valid = { desc = DISCRIMINATED_CULTURALLY }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name }
		}
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = daoyu_nul }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } } } desc = daoyu_has_only_one }#只有一个
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } } } desc = daoyu_has_over_one }#有多个
		}
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = daoyu_nul }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = concept_primary_culture }#主流文化
		}
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = daoyu_nul }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count = 0 } } } desc = daoyu_has_no }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count > 1 } } } desc = daoyu_has }
		}
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = daoyu_nul }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = DISCRIMINATED_CULTURALLY }#受歧视文化
		}
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.510 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.510 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_get_name
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:daoyu_target_country
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				is_ai = yes
				or = {
					and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } }
					and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count > 1 } }
					and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { set_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = daoyu_page_01 trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_root_get_name
		trigger = {
			or = {
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count > 1 } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } }
			}
		}
		set_variable = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = { set_variable = daoyu_page_01 trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
	}
}

daoyu.511 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = je_tutorial_increase_immigration#增加迁入移民
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { desc = concept_migration_target_desc }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_law_closed_borders
		trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country has_law = law_type:law_closed_borders } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { activate_law = law_type:law_no_migration_controls }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = law_no_migration_controls
		trigger = { has_law = law_type:law_closed_borders }
		activate_law = law_type:law_no_migration_controls
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_mass_migration_target#移民潮目的地
		trigger = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_closed_borders } exists = scope:daoyu_target_country scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_law = law_type:law_closed_borders } } any_scope_state = { state_is_eligible_as_mass_migration_target = yes } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { state_is_eligible_as_mass_migration_target = yes } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.512 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_m_cu
		every_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_from_diplomatic_actions } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.370 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}

	option = {
		name = daoyu_tst_7
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_7 }
		scope:daoyu_tst_7 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tst_8
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_8 }
		scope:daoyu_tst_8 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_tst_9
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_tst_9 }
		scope:daoyu_tst_9 = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
	}
	option = {
		name = NEXT_PAGE
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_variable = daoyu_return
		every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target }
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_1 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_2 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_3
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_4 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_5 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_6
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_7 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_8 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_9
		if = {
			limit = { any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target }
			ordered_scope_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } order_by = migration_pull }
			random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } set_variable = daoyu_target_country }
			set_variable = daoyu_page_01 trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes }
		}
		else = {
			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return } remove_variable = daoyu_return trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.512 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}

daoyu.520 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod
	flavor = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population } } desc = daoyu_root_get_name }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name }
		}
		first_valid = { desc = religious_orthodocy_enforced_mod }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }
			set_global_variable = daoyu_520
		}
		if = {
			limit= { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
			random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country#目标国家
		trigger = { nor = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion has_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population } }
		if = { limit = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } set_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population }
	}
	option = {
		name = catholic#天主教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "catholic" }
	}
	option = {
		name = protestant#新教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "protestant" }
	}
	option = {
		name = orthodox#东正教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "orthodox" }
	}
	option = {
		name = oriental_orthodox#东方正统教会
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "oriental_orthodox" }
	}
	option = {
		name = sunni#逊尼派
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "sunni" }
	}
	option = {
		name = shiite#什叶派
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "shiite" }
	}
	option = {
		name = ibadi#伊巴德派
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "ibadi" }
	}
	option = {
		name = jewish#犹太教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "jewish" }
	}
	option = {
		name = mahayana#大乘佛教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "mahayana" }
	}

		name = gelugpa#格鲁派

	}

		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "theravada" }
	}
	option = {

		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "confucian" }
	}
	option = {
		name = hindu#印度教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "hindu" }
	}
	option = {
		name = shinto#神道教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "shinto" }
	}
	option = {
		name = sikh#锡克教
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "sikh" }
	}
	option = {
		name = animist#泛灵论
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "animist" }
	}
	option = {
		name = atheist#无神论
		daoyu_religious_enforced_effect = { RELIGION = "atheist" }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_target_country_convert_population
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion not = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }
			set_global_variable = dculo_10
		}
		else = { remove_global_variable = daoyu_520 }
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_520 } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.520 popup = yes } }
		else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = dculo_10 } trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
		else = {
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes }
			#一球一族一教
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion not = { has_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } }
				every_scope_character = { change_character_culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture }
				daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
				add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture
				every_scope_state = {
					every_scope_pop = { if = { limit = { not = { culture = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture } } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture } } }
				}
				daoyu_remove_homeland_effect = yes
				every_scope_state = { state_region = { add_homeland = scope:daoyu_only_one_culture } }
				set_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion
				random_country = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.509 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

daoyu.570 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_mark_target_culture
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } desc = daoyu_mark_target_culture_get_name }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } desc = daoyu_mark_target_culture }
		}
	}
	flavor = daoyu_mark_target_culture_flavor
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete }
			set_global_variable = daoyu_save_mark_target_culture_effect
			daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_save_mark_target_culture_effect
		}
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_mark_target_culture#删除标记文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete
		set_global_variable = dculo_remove_global_variable_effect
		daoyu_all_culture_effect = yes
		remove_global_variable = dculo_remove_global_variable_effect
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_mark_target_culture#标记文化
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete } }
		hidden_effect = { set_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_begin trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_obsession#痴迷
		if = { limit = { not = { exists = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } custom_tooltip = daoyu_mark_target_culture custom_tooltip = NA hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } } }
		else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_obsession set_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_obsession hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.581 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_primary_culture_mark_target_culture_for_root#本国加入主流文化标记文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
		add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_primary_culture_change_into_mark_target_culture_for_root#标记文化同化本国主流文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = yes } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
		add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_owned_state_add_cultural_community#添加文化社群
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete any_scope_state = { not = { has_cultural_community = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = { not = { has_cultural_community = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } }
			add_cultural_community = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#目标地区
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.572 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_primary_culture_mark_target_culture_for_target_country#目标国家加入主流文化标记文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_primary_culture_change_into_mark_target_culture_for_target_country#标记文化同化目标国家主流文化
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country not = { country_has_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { pop_has_primary_culture = yes } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture } } }
			daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
			add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_mark_target_culture
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_state#目标国家的地区
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.571 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
	}
}

		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.581 popup = yes } }
	}

		name = daoyu_mark_target_culture#标记文化

		hidden_effect = { set_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_begin trigger_event = { id = dculo.10 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {

	}
