daoyu.590 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } not = { this = c:CHI } } } desc = daoyu_country_has_primary_culture_more_than_one } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } not = { this = c:CHI } } } desc = daoyu_line_reaks } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { this = root not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } } } desc = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country }
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:daoyu_target_country }
			scope:daoyu_target_country = {
				if = { limit = { this = c:CHI is_ai = yes } cu:han = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_culture } }
				else_if = { limit = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } } random_scope_culture = { limit = { is_primary_culture_of = root } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_culture } }
			}
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { religion = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_religion } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#民族同化
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } not = { this = c:CHI } } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state } }
		daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#民族同化
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { is_ai = yes this = c:CHI } }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state } }
		daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#民族同化#目标地区
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } this = root } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_states#民族同化#已整合地区
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } this = root } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_incorporated = yes } set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unincorporated_states#民族同化#未整合地区
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } this = root } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_incorporated = no } set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = battle_combat_effectiveness_owned_province_mult#民族同化#本国领土
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count = 1 } this = root } }
		every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_target_state }
		daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
	}
	after = {
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		clear_saved_scope = daoyu_target_country
		hidden_effect = {
			random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_300 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_300 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.300 popup = yes } }
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_500 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_500 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_600 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_600 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}

daoyu.600 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat

	flavor = daoyu_states_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = building_expanded_notification_group#扩建
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.602 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_building#拆除建筑

		else = { custom_tooltip = NONE custom_tooltip = POTENTIAL_BUILDINGS hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_each_culture_of_state#地区民族

	}

		name = concept_incorporate_state#整合地区

		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } } }
	}

		name = daoyu_united_all_state_culture_effect#一键洗地

	option = {
		name = move_capital_lens_option#迁都

		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count > 1 } } custom_tooltip = daoyu_multiple_target_state hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 is_capital = yes } } custom_tooltip = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } } }
		else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = move_market_capital_lens_option#迁移市场中心
		if = { limit = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } } custom_tooltip = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count > 1 } } custom_tooltip = daoyu_multiple_target_state hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } } }
		else_if = { limit = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 this = root.market_capital } } custom_tooltip = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } } }
		else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_move_market hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.601 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = good_pollution_modifier#污染治理措施

		else = { hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.604 popup = yes } } }

#地区
daoyu.601 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = STATES
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_capital_lens_option }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_market_capital_lens_option }
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_capital_lens_option } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } desc = move_market_capital_lens_option } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = FROM } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = daoyu_tst_1 } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = TO } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 } desc = daoyu_tst_2 } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
			random_scope_state = { limit = { is_capital = yes } save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_1 }
			random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_market any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
			random_scope_state = { limit = { this = root.market_capital } save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_1 }
			random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_tst_2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } exists = scope:daoyu_tst_2 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state is_incorporated = no } set_state_type = incorporated }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market }
			daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market = yes
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital_or_move_market
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_capital
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_move_market
		}
		trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes }
	}
}

		if = { limit = { not = { any_scope_building = { is_building_type = building_skyscraper } } } custom_tooltip = journal_entry_completed_notification_group custom_tooltip = je_skyscraper_construction hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.620 popup = yes } } }
		else = {

		}
	}

		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.602 popup = yes } }
	}

daoyu.650 = {

	duration = 0

			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_adventitious_options }
			any_state = {
				or = {
					has_modifier = daoyu_state_negative_birth_rate_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_state_positive_birth_rate_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_growth_mortality

					has_modifier = daoyu_decree_promote_social_mobility
					has_modifier = daoyu_throughput_add
					has_modifier = daoyu_goods_input_mult
					has_modifier = daoyu_decree_enlistment_efforts
				}
			}
		}

	flavor = daoyu_states_desc
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = battle_combat_effectiveness_owned_province_mult#本国领土
		trigger = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_state#已整合地区
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
			or = { any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult } }
		}
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_incorporated = yes } set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID#目标地区无效
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
			or = {
				not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
				and = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#目标地区
		trigger = {
			not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
			or = {
				and = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
				and = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { not = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_assimilation_mult } }
			every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier }
		}
		else = { every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } } set_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.655 popup = yes } }
	}
	any_scope_state = { or = { has_assimilating_pops = yes has_converting_pops = yes } }
	option = {
		name = 1x
		trigger = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_state_colony_growth any_scope_state = { has_variable = daoyu_state_modifier } } }
		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "1" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = 2x

		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "2" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {

		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "5" }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.650 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {

		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "20" }

		daoyu_state_add_modifier_effect = { MULTIPLIER = "30" }

daoyu.660 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_migration
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_migration_flavor }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = daoyu_line_reaks } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = daoyu_line_reaks } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } } desc = daoyu_line_reaks } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } } desc = daoyu_cross_border_migration } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } } } desc = TARGET_STATE_NOT_VALID } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/southamerica_factory_opening.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/southamerica/factory_opening"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_trade.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_state_1 }
		random_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state not = { this = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_state_2 }
		random_state = { limit = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } owner = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_target_state_1#失业
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { not = { this = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } add_pop_wealth = { wealth_distribution = { value = 5 } } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_unemployed_to_daoyu_target_country#失业人口送目标国家
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } any_scope_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } } }
		every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_country.capital } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_concentration_the_target_country_unemployed_to_target_state_1#目标国家失业人口来目标地区
		trigger = { any_state = { any_scope_pop = { is_employed = no } owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 }  }
		scope:daoyu_target_country = { every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { is_employed = no } move_pop = scope:daoyu_target_state_1 } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cross_border_migration#跨境移民
		trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 1 } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.661 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_migration_from_A_to_B#
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_from every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_migration_from_B_to_A#
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state count = 2 } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_2 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_from every_scope_culture = { set_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
		scope:daoyu_target_state_1 = { set_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}
}

			every_state = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } remove_global_variable = daoyu_660 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes }
		}
		else = { every_state = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.662 popup = yes } }
	}

		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_4 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_5 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_6
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_7 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_8 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tcu_9
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_665 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_665 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.665 popup = yes } }
		else = {
			scope:daoyu_migration_from = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { every_scope_culture = { remove_variable = daoyu_potential_target } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_666 }
				remove_global_variable = daoyu_666
				if = {
					limit = {
						scope:daoyu_migration_from = {
							any_scope_pop = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } save_temporary_scope_as = daoyu_any_pop }
							any_scope_pop = { culture = { has_variable = daoyu_target_culture } not = { religion = scope:daoyu_any_pop.religion } }
						}
					}
					trigger_event = { id = daoyu.666 popup = yes }
				}
				else = { set_global_variable = daoyu_from_665 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.667 popup = yes } }
			}
			else = {
				scope:daoyu_migration_from = { remove_variable = daoyu_migration_from } scope:daoyu_migration_go_to = { remove_variable = daoyu_migration_go_to }
				if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_660 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_660 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.660 popup = yes } }
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_662 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_662 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.662 popup = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
}

daoyu.670 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = {
		first_valid = {
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_nationalized_buildings } desc = daoyu_nationalized_buildings }
			triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building } desc = daoyu_remove_building }
		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } } desc = ACHIEVEMENTS_DISABLED_NO_HEADER } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } desc = ACHIEVEMENTS_ENABLED_NO_HEADER } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_buildings#所有建筑
		trigger = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building any_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.671 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = battle_combat_effectiveness_owned_province_mult#本国领土
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { any_scope_building = { daoyu_can_nationalized = yes } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_all_owned_state
		hidden_effect = {
			every_scope_building = { limit = { daoyu_can_nationalized = yes not = { has_modifier = daoyu_nationalized_buildings } } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_preselection_building days = 1 } }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.672 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_states#已整合地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = yes any_scope_building = { daoyu_can_nationalized = yes } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_incorporated_owned_state
		hidden_effect = {
			every_scope_building = { limit = { state = { is_incorporated = yes } daoyu_can_nationalized = yes not = { has_modifier = daoyu_nationalized_buildings } } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_preselection_building days = 1 } }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.672 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unincorporated_states#未整合地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { is_incorporated = no any_scope_building = { daoyu_can_nationalized = yes } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_unincorporated_owned_state
		hidden_effect = {
			every_scope_building = { limit = { state = { is_incorporated = no } daoyu_can_nationalized = yes not = { has_modifier = daoyu_nationalized_buildings } } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_preselection_building days = 1 } }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.672 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#目标地区
		trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state any_scope_building = { daoyu_can_nationalized = yes } } }
		set_variable = daoyu_target_state
		hidden_effect = {
			every_scope_building = { limit = { state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } daoyu_can_nationalized = yes not = { has_modifier = daoyu_nationalized_buildings } } add_modifier = { name = daoyu_preselection_building days = 1 } }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.672 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_nationalized_buildings
		remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.600 popup = yes } }
	}

#删除建筑
daoyu.671 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_remove_all_buildings
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = daoyu_target_country_additional } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_state = { owner = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { desc = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } } desc = ACHIEVEMENTS_DISABLED_NO_HEADER } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_scope_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } desc = ACHIEVEMENTS_ENABLED_NO_HEADER } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "votp_realist_household" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = GLOBAL_CULTURE#全球
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } }
		every_state = { set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_target_country_get_name
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country any_scope_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes } } }
		random_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_except_for_root
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } any_country = { is_ai = yes any_scope_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes } } }
		every_country = { limit = { is_ai = yes } every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } }
	}
	option = {
		name = battle_combat_effectiveness_owned_province_mult#本国领土
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } any_scope_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes } }
		every_scope_state = { set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_incorporated_states#已整合地区
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } any_scope_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes is_incorporated = yes } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_incorporated = yes } set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_unincorporated_states#未整合地区
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } any_scope_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes is_incorporated = no } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { is_incorporated = no } set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings }
	}
	option = {
		name = decree_daoyu_target_state#目标地区
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } any_scope_state = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_has_building_trigger = yes has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#
		trigger = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } }
		set_variable = daoyu_return
		hidden_effect = { daoyu_remove_all_buildings_effect = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = { limit = { any_state = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } } every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } remove_variable = daoyu_remove_all_buildings } }
		else = { set_variable = daoyu_return }
	}
	after = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return } remove_variable = daoyu_return trigger_event = { id = daoyu.670 popup = yes } }
		else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.671 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	type = country_event

	title = daoyu_cheat

		}
	}
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_all_owned_state } desc = battle_combat_effectiveness_owned_province_mult } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_incorporated_owned_state } desc = concept_incorporated_states } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_unincorporated_owned_state } desc = concept_unincorporated_states } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_target_state } desc = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/europenorthamerica_london_center.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/europenorthamerica/london_center"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_portrait.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { every_scope_building = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_nationalized_buildings or = { is_building_type = building_university is_building_type = building_government_administration } } remove_modifier = daoyu_nationalized_buildings } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_show_all#显示所有
		hidden_effect = {
			daoyu_set_change_option = yes
			every_scope_building = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_preselection_building } remove_modifier = daoyu_nationalized_buildings add_modifier = { name = daoyu_potential_building days = 1 } }
			daoyu_search_current_building = yes
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.675 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = URBAN_PART_OF_STATE#城镇建筑
		trigger = { any_scope_building = { daoyu_urban_building_trigger = yes } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_urban_building
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.673 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESOURCE#资源
		trigger = { any_scope_building = { daoyu_resources_building_trigger = yes } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_resource_building
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.673 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = AGRICULTURE#农业
		trigger = { any_scope_building = { daoyu_agriculture_building_trigger = yes } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_agriculture_building
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.673 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = INFRA_PART_OF_STATE#开发
		trigger = { any_scope_building = { daoyu_development_building_trigger = yes } }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_development_building
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.673 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_scope_building = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_preselection_building } remove_modifier = daoyu_preselection_building }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.670 popup = yes }
		}
	}
	after = {
		remove_variable = daoyu_all_owned_state
		remove_variable = daoyu_incorporated_owned_state
		remove_variable = daoyu_unincorporated_owned_state
		remove_variable = daoyu_target_state
	}
}

			remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_7 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_8 remove_global_variable = daoyu_tst_9

				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_building_state_trait }

daoyu.950 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	trigger = { is_ai = no }
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_country_add_radicals }
			trigger_event = { id = daoyu.950 months = 1 }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = no not = { top_overlord = root } }
				make_independent = yes
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes aggressive_diplomatic_plays_permitted = yes or = { any_scope_state = { count > 4 } country_rank >= rank_value:minor_power } }
				add_treasury = -1000000
				every_scope_state = { daoyu_add_radicals_in_state_effect = yes }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes country_rank = rank_value:great_power }
				trigger_event = { id = daoyu.951 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { owner = { or = { is_ai = no not = { country_rank = rank_value:great_power } } } has_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks }
				remove_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks activate_building = { building = building_barracks }
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_state = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks } remove_variable = daoyu_deactivate_barracks activate_building = { building = building_barracks } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_country_add_radicals_end }
				remove_global_variable = daoyu_country_add_radicals_end remove_global_variable = daoyu_all_AI_country
			}
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.392 popup = yes } }
		}
	}
}

			daoyu_remove_all_primary_culture_effect = yes
			add_primary_culture = scope:daoyu_target_culture
			every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { not = { culture = scope:daoyu_target_culture } } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_target_culture } } }
			every_scope_state = { convert_population = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_target_religion } }
		}
		else = {
			remove_primary_culture = cu:manchu
			if = { limit = { exists = c:TIB } annex = c:TIB }
			ruler = { religion = { save_scope_as = daoyu_target_religion } }
			every_scope_state = { every_scope_pop = { limit = { not = { culture = cu:han } } change_pop_culture = { value = 1 target = cu:han } } }
			every_scope_state = { convert_population = { value = 1 target = scope:daoyu_target_religion } }
		}
	}
}

	type = country_event
	placement = ROOT
	hidden = yes
	trigger = { is_ai = yes }

			limit = { or = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country_industry_banned has_variable = daoyu_target_country_extraction_economy } }

			if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country_extraction_economy  not = { has_law = law_type:law_extraction_economy } } activate_law = law_type:law_extraction_economy }

				if = { limit = { has_building = building_food_industry } remove_building = building_food_industry }

					random_scope_pop = { limit = { literacy_rate < 0.8 } set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = 0.85 } }
					random_scope_pop = { limit = { literacy_rate < 0.8 } set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = 0.85 } }
					random_scope_pop = { limit = { literacy_rate < 0.8 } set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = 0.85 } }
					random_scope_pop = { limit = { literacy_rate < 0.8 } set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = 0.85 } }
					random_scope_pop = { limit = { literacy_rate < 0.8 } set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = 0.85 } }
					random_scope_pop = { limit = { literacy_rate < 0.8 } set_pop_literacy = { literacy_rate = 0.85 } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_auto_bureaucracy_authority_influence }
				set_variable = { name = daoyu_bureaucracy_usage_var value = 0 }
				set_variable = { name = daoyu_authority_usage_var value = 0 }
				set_variable = { name = daoyu_influence_usage_var value = 0 }
				if = {
					limit = { bureaucracy_usage > var:daoyu_bureaucracy_usage_var }
					while = { count = 1000 if = { limit = { bureaucracy_usage > var:daoyu_bureaucracy_usage_var } change_variable = { name = daoyu_bureaucracy_usage_var add = 100 } } }
					remove_modifier = daoyu_auto_country_bureaucracy add_modifier = { name = daoyu_auto_country_bureaucracy multiplier = var:daoyu_bureaucracy_usage_var }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { authority_usage > var:daoyu_authority_usage_var }
					while = { count = 1000 if = { limit = { authority_usage > var:daoyu_authority_usage_var } change_variable = { name = daoyu_authority_usage_var add = 100 } } }
					remove_modifier = daoyu_auto_country_influence add_modifier = { name = daoyu_auto_country_influence multiplier = var:daoyu_authority_usage_var }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { influence_usage > var:daoyu_influence_usage_var }
					while = { count = 1000 if = { limit = { influence_usage > var:daoyu_influence_usage_var } change_variable = { name = daoyu_influence_usage_var add = 100 } } }
					remove_modifier = daoyu_auto_country_influence add_modifier = { name = daoyu_auto_country_influence multiplier = var:daoyu_influence_usage_var }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes has_global_variable = daoyu_996_on }
			random_country = { limit = { is_ai = no } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.996 } }
			daoyu_remove_all_country_modifier_effect = yes
			daoyu_state_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
			every_country = {
				every_interest_group = {
					if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval } remove_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_approval }
					if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str } remove_modifier = daoyu_interest_group_pol_str }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#option = { }
}
